TABLE: public.action_type
============================================================

COLUMNS:
  action_type: character varying NOT NULL
  description: character varying NOT NULL
  parent_type: character varying NULL

TOTAL ROWS: 35

SAMPLE DATA (5 rows):

Row 1:
  action_type: ACTIVATOR
  description: Positively effects the normal functioning of the protein e.g., activation of an enzyme or cleaving a clotting protein precursor
  parent_type: POSITIVE MODULATOR

Row 2:
  action_type: AGONIST
  description: Binds to and activates a receptor, often mimicking the effect of the endogenous ligand
  parent_type: POSITIVE MODULATOR

Row 3:
  action_type: ALLOSTERIC ANTAGONIST
  description: Binds to a receptor at an allosteric site and prevents activation by a positive allosteric modulator at that site
  parent_type: NEGATIVE MODULATOR

Row 4:
  action_type: ANTAGONIST
  description: Binds to a receptor and prevents activation by an agonist through competing for the binding site
  parent_type: NEGATIVE MODULATOR

Row 5:
  action_type: ANTISENSE INHIBITOR
  description: Prevents translation of a complementary mRNA sequence through binding and targeting it for degradation
  parent_type: NEGATIVE MODULATOR
